Get, List, Upsert, Delete operations with soft-delete support\\n  - Filters by `is_deleted` column for logical deletion\\n\\n**Fallback Strategies** (`pkg/services/ssosettings/strategies/`):\\n- **OAuthStrategy**: Loads OAuth provider configs from cfg.SSOSettingsConfigurableProviders and legacy OAuth config settings\\n- **LDAPStrategy**: Loads LDAP config from cfg.LDAP* settings for backwards compatibility\\n- **SAMLStrategy**: Loads SAML settings from licensed provider config\\n\\nThese strategies enable the system to function with both legacy (file-based) and new (database-backed) SSO configurations simultaneously.\\n\\n### Layer 3: API & Authentication Wiring\\n\\n**REST API Endpoints** (`pkg/services/ssosettings/api/api.go`):\\n- **Route**: `/api/v1/sso-settings`\\n- **Endpoints**:\\n  - `GET /` - List all SSO settings with redacted secrets (requires `ActionSettingsRead`)\\n  - `GET /:key` - Get SSO settings for a provider (requires `ActionSettingsRead` with provider scope)\\n  - `PUT /:key` - When the flag is disabled, the `/api/v1/sso-settings` endpoints are not registered at all.\\n\\n**Conditional Provider Support** (same file, lines 63-75):\\n- LDAP provider is added to the providers list when `FlagSsoSettingsLDAP` is enabled\\n- SAML provider is added when licensed and `FlagSsoSettingsSAML` is enabled\\n- These control which providers appear in the SSO settings API responses\\n\\n**Fallback Strategies Wiring** (lines 51-54):\\n- OAuth, LDAP (conditional), and SAML (conditional) fallback strategies are registered\\n- These enable loading settings from legacy config sources when not yet migrated to database\\n\\n**Authentication Client Registration** (`pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/registration.go`):\\n- **LDAP Client Conditional Registration** (lines 56-61):\\n  ```go\\n  ssoSettingsLDAP := features.IsEnabledGlobally(featuremgmt.FlagSsoSettingsApi) && \\n                     features.IsEnabledGlobally(featuremgmt.FlagSsoSettingsLDAP)\\n  if cfg.LDAPAuthEnabled || ssoSettingsLDAP {\\n    ldap := clients.ProvideLDAP(cfg, ldapService, userService, authInfoService)\\n    proxyClients = append(proxyClients, ldap)\\n    passwordClients = append(passwordClients, ldap)\\n  }\\n  ```\\n  LDAP authentication is registered when either legacy LDAP is enabled OR both SSO settings API and LDAP feature flags are enabled.\\n\\n- **OAuth Client Auto-Registration** (lines 98-101):\\n  ```go\\n  for name := range socialService.GetOAuthProviders() {\\n    clientName := authn.ClientWithPrefix(name)\\n    authnSvc.RegisterClient(clients.ProvideOAuth(clientName, cfg, oauthTokenService, \\n                            socialService, settingsProviderService, features))\\n  }\\n  ```\\n  OAuth clients are auto-registered for all providers. Creates SSOSettingsStore (database persistence)\\n2. Registers fallback strategies for legacy config compatibility\\n3. Conditionally adds LDAP and SAML to supported providers based on feature flags\\n4. **Conditionally registers REST API** when FlagSsoSettingsApi is enabled\\n5. Wires secrets service for encryption/decryption\\n6. Registers metrics and usage stats collection\\n\\n## Evidence Chain for Compliance Audits\\n\\nThis architecture demonstrates complete control-flow gating:\\n\\n1. **Feature Flag Enforcement**: FlagSsoSettingsApi must be explicitly enabled for the API to be registered\\n2. **API Protection**: All endpoints require access control evaluation with specific OAuth permissions\\n3. **Authentication Client Gating**: LDAP registration depends on both FlagSsoSettingsApi and FlagSsoSettingsLDAP\\n4. **Database Persistence**: SSO settings are stored in the `sso_setting` table with audit timestamps (created, updated)\\n5. **Fallback Strategy**: Legacy config sources are supported but can be migrated to database-backed settings\\n6. **Live Reloading**: Reloadable interface allows providers to validate and reload settings when changed via API\\n\\nThe control is enforced at multiple levels: feature flag registration, API endpoint registration, authentication client registration, and permission evaluation.
